posted:Posted June 16, 2023
msg:We've stayed here pre-pandemic and back then it was really good. You would see their attention to service and details.

First time back since pandemic and boy did it become so horrible! It doesn't even feel like a part of Marriott group, instead a locally chinese run and owned hotel.

- The room smells. The only toiletries they give you is a toothbrush and a soap. IT WAS EXTREMELY HOT because the AC was controlled centrally by the hotel. Why not let each resident decide the room temp on their own?! I might've understood this if it was in the winter, but it was summer and 30 deg celcius outside! They didn't have a refrigerator, they had one with lights on pretending to be one. When I called the front desk why the refrigerator is not even a bit cold, he said that "it wasn't like those refrigerators that cools because people don't like cold, it's the same in all rooms". This is the first time I've encountered a fake ref let alone in a 5 star hotel like Marriott.

- Breakfast is terrible. Avoid it like the plague. It's so dirty in there, the used tables are wiped with a dirty rag. The servers had a sprayer with disinfectant but they never once used it. In all 4 days of stay not a single dish was changed. Not much selection for foreigners, mostly catering to the locals with hard boiled egg, congee and noodle soup.
‚Ä¢ One time a group of men started smoking inside the dining breakfast area. We told the wait staff and pointed to the "no smoking" sign. She said "how could I tell them to stop?". So we told her to call the manager and she just told us to move to another table. Like what?!

- Here comes the highlight of our stay. I booked and paid in full via trip.com. I have all proof, e-receipt and booking confirmation. Upon check-in they swiped my credit card for the deposit. This is fine and normal. Upon check-out nothing was said by the receptionist except everything was good to go. Then lo and behold days after when I'm back home in my country, I see that they charged my CC AGAIN for the room?! I emailed them several times and they NEVER REPLIED. Luckily, we have an agent based in Yiwu who I asked to call them. She was able to get their invoice and now we have proof that they DID CHARGE ME FOR THE STAY EVEN IF I'M FULLY PAID WITH TRIP.COM. Now it's been more than a week and they keep giving excuses why they cannot refund it yet. (One was my bank rejected the credit. What kind of a bank rejects a credit?! My bank says not a single attempt was made for any credit). I have resorted to filling a dispute with my CC but it could get rejected. THIS IS SO MUCH OF A HASSLE. 

NEVER STAYING HERE EVER AGAIN
